###- Section 00: Namespaces -###
add_namespace = YUN.introgame #YUN introgame
add_namespace = YUN.earlygame #YUN earlygame

###- Section 01: Intro Game -###

##Section 1a (000-399): Introgame Political Events

#YUN Internal Event Chain (000-049):

country_event = { #Hidden event to take away research slot
	id = YUN.introgame.000

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.introgame.000 option 1"
		add_research_slot = -1
	}
}

country_event = { #The Scheming Court in the Southwest
	id = YUN.introgame.001
	title = YUN.introgame.001.t
	desc = YUN.introgame.001.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_YUN_tang_jiyao_and_generals

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by [HISTORY FILE] #Fires January 04 1936

	trigger = {
		YUN_is_phase_1_trigger = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = YUN.introgame.002 days = 14 } #Dian-Gui Border Tensions
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.introgame.001 option YUN.introgame.001.a"
		name = YUN.introgame.001.a #Our discussions will be fruitful I’m sure.
		custom_effect_tooltip = YUN.introgame.001_tt
	}
}

country_event = { #Dian-Qian Border Tensions
	id = YUN.introgame.002
	title = YUN.introgame.002.t
	desc = YUN.introgame.002.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_YUN_yunnan_troops_7

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by [EVENT] YUN.introgame.001 #The Scheming Court in the Southwest // Fires January 18 1936
	trigger = {
		YUN_is_phase_1_trigger = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.introgame.002 option YUN.introgame.002.a"
		name = YUN.introgame.002.a #One day, we shall return to Guizhou.
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		YUN_introminigame_add_UPC_small_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.introgame.002 option YUN.introgame.002.b"
		name = YUN.introgame.002.b #One day, we shall leave Guizhou.
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		YUN_introminigame_add_KMT_small_effect = yes
	}

	after = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = YUN.introgame.002_tt
		set_country_flag = YUN_introgame_minigame_start_flag
	}
}

	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.introgame.004 option YUN.introgame.004.b"
		name = YUN.introgame.004.b #Reform of the economy will save it.
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		YUN_introminigame_add_UPC_small_effect = yes
	}

	after = {
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = YUN_unrest_in_kunming_level_1
			add_idea = YUN_unrest_in_kunming_level_2
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = YUN_abysmal_economy_idea1
			add_idea = YUN_abysmal_economy_idea2
		}
		complete_national_focus = YUN_maintaining_the_paradigm
	}
}

country_event = { #Tang Jiyao’s Gambit
	id = YUN.introgame.006
	title = YUN.introgame.006.t
	desc = YUN.introgame.006.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_YUN_tang_jiyao_painting

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by [EVENT] GXC.introgame.150 #Liangguang Devolves Into Civil War // March 02 1936
	trigger = {
		YUN_is_phase_1_trigger = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = YUN.introgame.007 days = 30 } #The Exiles in Guizhou

			activate_mission = YUN_introminigame_war_preparation_mission_timer
			activate_mission = YUN_troops_flood_to_the_border_monthly_timer
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = YUN decision = YUN_introminigame_switch_sides_decision }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = YUN decision = YUN_introminigame_commence_the_assault_decision }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = YUN decision = YUN_introminigame_accelerate_our_buildup_decision }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = YUN decision = YUN_introminigame_develop_our_battleplan_decision }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = YUN decision = YUN_introminigame_win_the_war_of_wills_decision }

			#Send Events to other tags
			#HNN and GXC get their events triggered in their files.
			SZC = { country_event = { id = YUN.introgame.060 days = 7 random_days = 93 } } #Our Interests in Dian-Qian
			CHI = { country_event = { id = YUN.introgame.065 days = 7 random_days = 93 } } #Distant Leftists in the Southwest Struggle
			GEA = { country_event = { id = YUN.introgame.070 days = 7 random_days = 93 } } #German Interests in the Dian-Qian Showdown
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.introgame.006 option YUN.introgame.006.a"
		name = YUN.introgame.006.a #Guizhou this year, Guangzhou the next, and one day all of China!
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				#Rig it if you set gamerules so they will always win.
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_PATH option = YUN_PATH_SOCCON }
			}
		}
		YUN_introminigame_add_UPC_medium_effect = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = YUN.introgame.006.a_tt
		#By default you will be playing as UPC
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.introgame.006 option YUN.introgame.006.b"
		name = YUN.introgame.006.b #They shall not pass!
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				#Rig it if you set gamerules so they will always win.
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_PATH option = YUN_PATH_AUTDEM }
			}
		}
		YUN_introminigame_add_KMT_medium_effect = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = YUN.introgame.006.b_tt
		set_country_flag = YUN_introminigame_playing_as_KMT_flag
	}
}

country_event = { #Hunan’s Stake in Guizhou
	id = YUN.introgame.011
	title = YUN.introgame.011.t
	desc = {
		text = YUN.introgame.011.HNN_ruled_by_KMT
		trigger = {
			HNN = { china_is_aligned_with_kmt = yes }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = YUN.introgame.011.HNN_ruled_by_non_KMT
		trigger = {
			HNN = { china_is_aligned_with_kmt = no }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_HNN_yuan_zuming_figure_2

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by [EVENT] YUN.introgame.010 #Long Yun’s Report // August 02 1936.
	trigger = {
		YUN_is_phase_1_trigger = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = YUN.introgame.012 days = 30 } #The Intellectuals Weigh In
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.introgame.011 option YUN.introgame.011.a"
		name = YUN.introgame.011.a #He Yingqin and Lu Tao are able to come to a (temporary) arrangement.
		trigger = {
			HNN = { china_is_aligned_with_kmt = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 20 }
		YUN_introminigame_add_KMT_medium_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.introgame.011 option YUN.introgame.011.b"
		name = YUN.introgame.011.b #Tensions with Hunan distract Kuomintang troops from the border.
		ai_chance = { base = 20 }
		if = {
			limit = { HNN = { china_is_aligned_with_kmt = yes } }
			add_stability = -0.03
		}
		else = {
			YUN_introminigame_add_UPC_medium_effect = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.introgame.011 option YUN.introgame.011.c"
		name = YUN.introgame.011.c #The Yunnan Clique hardly needs Yuan to take Guizhou.
		ai_chance = { base = 60 }
		trigger = {
			HNN = { china_is_aligned_with_kmt = no }
		}
		add_war_support = -0.03
	}
}

country_event = { #The Guizhou Connection [GXC POV Event]
	id = YUN.introgame.050
	title = YUN.introgame.050.t
	desc = YUN.introgame.050.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GXC_bai_li_and_huang

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by [EVENT] GXC.introgame.009 #A War on Two Fronts
	trigger = {
		YUN_is_phase_1_trigger = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.introgame.050 option YUN.introgame.050.a"
		name = YUN.introgame.050.a #The 7th Army pulls their men from Guizhou.
		ai_chance = { base = 80 }
		add_manpower = 3000
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.introgame.050 option YUN.introgame.050.b"
		name = YUN.introgame.050.b #Li’s supply lines remain open, aiding the KMT.
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		add_war_support = -0.03
		YUN = { effect_tooltip = { YUN_introminigame_add_KMT_large_effect = yes } }
		hidden_effect = {
			YUN = { country_event = { id = YUN.introgame.052 days = 3 } } #Nationalist Cross-Border Supply Lines
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.introgame.050 option YUN.introgame.050.c"
		name = YUN.introgame.050.c #New Guangxi pulls their share from the stockpiles.
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		add_political_power = -30
		YUN = { effect_tooltip = { YUN_introminigame_add_UPC_large_effect = yes } }
		hidden_effect = {
			YUN = { country_event = { id = YUN.introgame.053 days = 3 } } #Revolutionary Brotherhood and the Revolutionary Army
		}
	}
}

#YUN Resolution Event Chain (100-149):
country_event = { #The Late-Autumn Offensive
	id = YUN.introgame.100
	title = YUN.introgame.100.t
	desc = YUN.introgame.100.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_YUN_NRA_soldiers_4

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by [EVENT] DECISION #YUN_troops_flood_to_the_border_monthly_timer // November 02 1936
	trigger = {
		YUN_is_phase_1_trigger = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.introgame.100 option YUN.introgame.100.a"
		name = YUN.introgame.100.a #Come what may, we shall prevail.
	   #Well, this is how the Ai will basically always do the mini-game, we'll rig it so it's about 50/50 with weights if YUN got external support.
		add_war_support = -0.25
		add_stability = -0.25
		add_manpower = -25000
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_PATH option = YUN_PATH_SOCCON }
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_PATH option = YUN_PATH_SOCCON }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = YUN_introgame_minigame_rigged_warning_tt
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				#YUN will generally go the way the player wants to even if they had massive skill issue.
				modifier = {
					factor = 3
					is_ai = no
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = YUN_introminigame_playing_as_KMT_flag
					}
				}
				#YUN will try to be the same alignment usually as HNN and GXC
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					GXC = { china_alignment_federalists = yes }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					HNN = { china_alignment_federalists = yes }
				}
				#You get a 1.5x (about a 10% boost the first time, with diminishing returns) for each external backer you got. Mechanically it means you have a friend. HNN, GXC, SZC, and GEA may support UPC.
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					check_variable = { YUN.YUN_UPC_introminigame_external_help_var > 0 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					check_variable = { YUN.YUN_UPC_introminigame_external_help_var > 1 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					check_variable = { YUN.YUN_UPC_introminigame_external_help_var > 2 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					check_variable = { YUN.YUN_UPC_introminigame_external_help_var > 3 }
				}
				modifier = {
					#Rig it if you set gamerules so they will always win.
					factor = 0
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_PATH option = YUN_PATH_SOCCON }
				}
				country_event = { id = YUN.introgame.101 days = 7 } #The Yunnan Army Overruns Guizhou
			}
			50 = {
				#YUN will generally go the way the player wants to even if they had massive skill issue.
				modifier = {
					factor = 3
					is_ai = no
					has_country_flag = YUN_introminigame_playing_as_KMT_flag
				}
				#YUN will try to be the same alignment usually as HNN and GXC
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					GXC = {
						OR = {
							china_alignment_left_kuomintang = yes
							china_alignment_right_kuomintang = yes
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					HNN = {
						OR = {
							china_alignment_left_kuomintang = yes
							china_alignment_right_kuomintang = yes
						}
					}
				}
				#You get a 1.5x (about a 10% boost the first time, with diminishing returns) for each external backer you got. Mechanically it means you have a friend. HNN, GXC, SZC, and CHI may support KMT.
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					check_variable = { YUN.YUN_KMT_introminigame_external_help_var > 0 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					check_variable = { YUN.YUN_KMT_introminigame_external_help_var > 1 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					check_variable = { YUN.YUN_KMT_introminigame_external_help_var > 2 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					check_variable = { YUN.YUN_KMT_introminigame_external_help_var > 3 }
				}
				modifier = {
					#Rig it if you set gamerules so they will always win.
					factor = 0
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_PATH option = YUN_PATH_AUTDEM }
				}
				country_event = { id = YUN.introgame.102 days = 7 } #The Zhaotong Incident
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = YUN.earlygame.400 #A Nationalist Junta in the Southwest
	title = YUN.earlygame.400.t
	desc = YUN.earlygame.400.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_YUN_he_yingqin_and_zhu_peide

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by EVENT: YUN.introgame.102

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "KR_Event_Logging;YUN GAME PROGRESS - YUN KMT Other"
			set_country_flag = YUN_phase_2_begins_flag
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			YUN_kmt_recruit_characters_effect = yes
			YUN_KMT_set_initial_parties = yes
			every_character = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_character_flag = YUN_BEI_character_flag
						has_character_flag = YUN_TJY_character_flag
						has_character_flag = HNN_fed_loyalist_flag
					}
				}
				retire = yes
			}
			activate_advisor = YUN_long_yun_sic
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_conservative
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			complete_national_focus = YUN_resurgence_of_the_kuomintang
			set_cosmetic_tag = YUN_KMT
			#Promote the Junta to Field Marshal Roles
			YUN_zhu_peide = { promote_leader = yes }
			YUN_he_yingqin = { promote_leader = yes }
			complete_national_focus = YUN_kunming_to_guiyang
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.earlygame.400 option YUN.earlygame.400.a"
		name = YUN.earlygame.400.a #The consolidation of Yunnan is the primary concern of the Kuomintang!

		YUN_3AL_small_effect = yes

			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_zhu_peide
				ideology = social_conservative_subtype
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = focus_tree_will_change_tt
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:radical_socialist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:paternal_autocrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = YUN.earlygame.4000 #Kuomintang Forces Invade Yunnan!
		}
	}
}

	}
	desc = {
		text = YUN.earlygame.811.d.whitepeace_and_lose_guizhou
		trigger = {
			YUN_GXC_war_lose_guizhou_trigger = yes
			YUN_GXC_war_become_satellite_trigger = no
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = YUN.earlygame.811.d.whitepeace_and_keep_guizhou
		trigger = {
			YUN_GXC_war_lose_guizhou_trigger = no
			YUN_GXC_war_become_satellite_trigger = no
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_YUN_long_yun_4

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by [DECISION]: YUN_accept_yunnans_surrender_decision

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			#Gotta swap out the characters before the puppet effect or else it will trigger satellite content for KMT/UPC
			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_long_yun
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_hu_ruoyu
				ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
			}
			activate_advisor = YUN_hu_ruoyu_sic
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = YUN_long_yun_clique_party_long
				name = YUN_long_yun_clique_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = YUN_republicans_party_long
				name = YUN_republicans_party
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = YUN_SCPC_KMT }
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes #Just in case the YUN_KMT cosmetic tag isn't already dropped.
				set_cosmetic_tag = YUN_SCPC_UPC
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = YUN_KMT }
				#Don't drop SCPC
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.earlygame.811 option YUN.earlygame.811.a"
		name = YUN.earlygame.811.a #A bitter defeat.
		#Lose Guizhou before peace-out transfer back control
		if = {
			limit = {
				YUN_GXC_war_lose_guizhou_trigger = yes
			}
			1051 = {
				#Guiyang
				controller = {
					transfer_state = 1051
				}
			}
			1051 = {
				#Zunyi
				controller = {
					transfer_state = 603
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				YUN_GXC_war_become_satellite_trigger = yes
			}
			FROM = { china_puppet_ROOT_effect = yes }
		}
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					owns_state = 594 #Nanning
					is_ally_with = var:594.owner #Nanning
				}
			}
			white_peace = YUN #YUN should not have any puppets at this phase
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = YUN
				relation = non_aggression_pact
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			YUN_GXC_clear_mechanic_effect = yes
			country_event = { id = YUN.midgame.700 days = 3 } #The Kunming Coup
		}
	}
}

		YUN_PSC_large_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = YUN_chose_the_public_security_bureau_flag
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc_lar = no }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_ideas = YUN_bureau_of_public_safety
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_intelligence_agency = no }
			create_intelligence_agency = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_form_department } }
			upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_form_department
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_psycho_warfare } }
			upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_psycho_warfare
		}
		else = { add_political_power = 50 }
	}
	option = { #Empower Chen Lifu's BIS
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.midgame.455 option YUN.midgame.455.b"
		name = YUN.midgame.455.b
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		#need ai weights later
		YUN_CCC_large_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = YUN_chose_bis_flag
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc_lar = no }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_ideas = YUN_bis_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_intelligence_agency = no }
			create_intelligence_agency = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_army_department } }
			upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_army_department
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_invisible_ink } }
			upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_invisible_ink
		}
		else = { add_political_power = 50 }
	}
	option = { #Go with Tewu
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.midgame.455 option YUN.midgame.455.c"
		name = YUN.midgame.455.c
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		#need ai weights later
		YUN_BSS_large_effect = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = YUN_chose_tewu_flag
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc_lar = no }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_ideas = YUN_tewu_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_intelligence_agency = no }
			create_intelligence_agency = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_commando_training } }
			upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_commando_training
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_passive_defense } }
			upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_passive_defense
		}
		else = { add_political_power = 50 }

country_event = { #Zhu Peide Purges Long Yun
	id = YUN.midgame.500
	desc = YUN.midgame.500.d
	title = YUN.midgame.500.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_YUN_long_yun_1
	is_triggered_only = yes #Fired 3 days after [EVENT]: china_events.5 OR china_events.7 - surrendering to RKT or LKT

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = YUN.midgame.501 days = 160 random_days = 40 } #Li Genyuan’s Second Chance

			set_country_flag = YUN_phase_3_begins_flag
			complete_national_focus = YUN_begin_grand_southern_reconstruction_project

			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_hu_ruoyu
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = YUN_garrison_commanders_party_long
				name = YUN_garrison_commanders_party
			}

			if = {
				limit = { overlord = { tag = CHI } }
				country_event = { id = YUN.midgame.520 days = 30 } #PAC Advisors Arrive in Kunming
				CHI = { country_event = { id = YUN.midgame.520 days = 30 } }
				log = "KR_Event_Logging;YUN GAME PROGRESS - YUN KMT Submits to LKT"
			}
			else = {
				log = "KR_Event_Logging;YUN GAME PROGRESS - YUN KMT Submits to RKT"
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.midgame.500 option YUN.midgame.500.a"
		name = YUN.midgame.500.a #Long Yun will remain in custody in Kunming.
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		YUN_long_yun = { retire = yes }
		YUN_3AR_large_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.midgame.500 option YUN.midgame.500.b"
		name = YUN.midgame.500.b #Long Yun will be transferred to house arrest in Mengze.
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		add_stability = -0.10
		YUN_HRY_large_effect = yes
	}

	after = {
		activate_advisor = YUN_li_genyuan_sic
		custom_effect_tooltip = focus_tree_will_change_tt
		set_country_flag = YUN_KMT_satellite_narrative_flag
		complete_national_focus = YUN_kuomintangising_the_southwest
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = YUN.midgame.700 #The Kunming Coup
	title = YUN.midgame.700.t
	desc = YUN.midgame.700.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_YUN_long_yun_horse

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by [EVENT] YUN.earlygame.811
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "KR_Event_Logging;YUN GAME PROGRESS - YUN NPA Other"
			country_event = { id = YUN.midgame.730 days = 160 random_days = 40 } #The Long Yun Clique
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = YUN_long_yun_clique_party_long
				name = YUN_long_yun_clique_party

			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = YUN_hu_ruoyu_clique_party_long #Will flip to Mengzi later
				name = YUN_hu_ruoyu_clique_party #Will flip to Mengzi later
			}
			end_coalition = yes
			YUN_lu_han = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			YUN_UPC_recruit_characters_effect = yes #Bring the UPC people back for now in case the KMT initally take over, then we'll purge them later in the event chain.
			YUN_3AL_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
			YUN_CEC_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
			YUN_PSC_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes

			YUN_CCC_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
			YUN_WPC_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
			YUN_BSS_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
			YUN_transition_to_NPA_pop_support_effect = yes
			YUN_transition_to_NPA_army_tree_effect = yes
			YUN_zhu_de = { retire = yes }
			YUN_chen_cheng = { retire = yes }

			YUN_dai_jitao = { retire = yes }

		}
	}

	option = { #An ignominious failure.

				character = YUN_long_yun
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_hu_ruoyu
				ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
			}

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = YUN_long_yun_clique_party_long
				name = YUN_long_yun_clique_party
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = YUN_phase_3_begins_flag
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = focus_tree_will_change_tt
		set_country_flag = YUN_NPA_satellite_narrative_flag
		complete_national_focus = YUN_to_save_yunnan_from_itself
		complete_national_focus = YUN_begin_grand_southern_reconstruction_project
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = YUN.midgame.701 #Yunnan Generals Stage Coup in Kunming

		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = YUN.lategame.412 #Zhang Qun’s Audacious Gambit
	title = YUN.lategame.412.t
	desc = YUN.lategame.412.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_YUN_zhang_qun_1

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by EVENT: YUN.lategame.411

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = YUN.lategame.413 days = 5 } #Dai Jitao and the CC Clique Plot
			YUN_zhang_qun = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			YUN_yang_yongtai = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.lategame.412 option YUN.lategame.412.a"
		name = YUN.lategame.412.a #The Political Science Clique makes yet another bid for power.
		promote_character = {
			character = YUN_zhang_qun
			ideology = market_liberal_subtype
		}
		activate_advisor = YUN_yang_yongtai_sic
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = market_liberal
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		set_variable = { YUN_PSC_aligned_delegates_variable = 502 } #Start with 502
		multiply_variable = { YUN_PSC_aligned_delegates_variable = ROOT.party_popularity@market_liberal } #502 x Market Liberal Popularity, ranges from 0-502.
		round_variable = YUN_PSC_aligned_delegates_variable #Makes sure its a nice, even number
		clamp_variable = {
			var = YUN_PSC_aligned_delegates_variable
			min = 0 #Can't have negative delegates
			max = 200 #You can have up to 40% of delegates aligned to you at the start.
		}
		#Rig it if you have game rules on
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_KMT_path option = YUN_KMT_PATH_QUN_MARLIB }
			}
			set_variable = { YUN_PSC_aligned_delegates_variable = 502 } #Start with 502
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHN_game_rule_rigged_warning_tt
		}

		custom_effect_tooltip = YUN_zhang_qun_gambit_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			#Activate decisions
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = YUN_Pass_the_Provisional_Constitution_decision }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = YUN_Loyalty_Tests_in_the_Bureaucracy_decision }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = YUN_Promise_a_Constitutional_government_decision }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = YUN_Release_Political_Prisoners_decision }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = YUN_Bribe_Miliitary_Officers_decision }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = YUN_Negotiate_with_the_SCPC_decision }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = YUN_Handle_the_Leftist_Bloc_decision }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = YUN_Negotiate_with_the_Dangwai_decision }
		}
	}
}

		multiply_variable = { YUN_CCC_aligned_delegates_variable = ROOT.party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat } #502 x Auth Dem Popularity, ranges from 0-502.
		round_variable = YUN_CCC_aligned_delegates_variable #Makes sure its a nice, even number
		clamp_variable = {
			var = YUN_CCC_aligned_delegates_variable
			min = 0 #Can't have negative delegates
			max = 200 #You can have up to 40% of delegates aligned to you at the start.
		}
		#Rig it if you have game rules on
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_KMT_path option = YUN_KMT_PATH_LIFU_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_KMT_path option = YUN_KMT_PATH_JITAO_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { YUN_CCC_aligned_delegates_variable = 502 } #Start with 502
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHN_game_rule_rigged_warning_tt
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = YUN_dai_jitao_and_the_CC_clique_plot_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			#Activate decisions
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = YUN_Call_a_Vote_of_No_Confidence_decision }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = YUN_Increase_Propaganda_Output_decision }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = YUN_Stoke_Xenophobic_Hysteria_decision }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = YUN_Orchestrate_a_Walkout_of_the_Bureaucracy_decision }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = YUN_Mobilise_the_Political_Commissars_decision }
		}
	}
}

	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.lategame.416 option YUN.lategame.416.a"
		name = YUN.lategame.416.a #Their praise is most appreciated.
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = { china_same_alignment_as_FROM = yes } #PREV is RKMT
			set_temp_variable = { YUN_PSC_delegate_change_temp_var = 0.10 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = yes } #LKMT or Republicans
			set_temp_variable = { YUN_PSC_delegate_change_temp_var = 0.05 }
		}
		else = {
			#Everyone else
			set_temp_variable = { YUN_PSC_delegate_change_temp_var = 0.03 }
		}
		YUN_KMT_hu_hanmin_crisis_PSC_delegates_effect = yes
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.lategame.416 option YUN.lategame.416.b"
		name = YUN.lategame.416.b #They will not be allowed to lead others to their folly.
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = { china_same_alignment_as_FROM = yes } #PREV is RKMT
			add_political_power = -100
			add_stability = -0.10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = yes } #LKMT or Republicans
			add_political_power = -50
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
		else = {
			#Everyone else
			add_political_power = -30
			add_stability = -0.03
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHN_fuel_to_civil_war_warning_tt
		hidden_effect = { FROM = { country_event = { id = YUN.lategame.419 days = 3 } } } #Our Votes Nullified
	}
}

		add_to_temp_variable = { YUN_combined_leftist_popularity_temp_var = ROOT.party_popularity@radical_socialist }
		add_to_temp_variable = { YUN_combined_leftist_popularity_temp_var = ROOT.party_popularity@social_democrat }
		add_to_temp_variable = { YUN_combined_leftist_popularity_temp_var = ROOT.party_popularity@social_liberal }

		set_temp_variable = { YUN_PSC_delegate_change_temp_var = YUN_combined_leftist_popularity_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { YUN_PSC_delegate_change_temp_var = -0.25 } #Soc Dem makes this decision potentially a lot so gonna guage it a bit so its only a quarter.
		YUN_KMT_hu_hanmin_crisis_PSC_delegates_effect = yes
		set_temp_variable = { YUN_CCC_delegate_change_temp_var = YUN_combined_leftist_popularity_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { YUN_CCC_delegate_change_temp_var = -0.25 } #Soc Dem makes this decision potentially a lot so gonna guage it a bit so its only a quarter.
		YUN_KMT_hu_hanmin_crisis_CCC_delegates_effect = yes
		set_temp_variable = { YUN_whampoa_coup_mission_timer_change_temp_var = ROOT.party_popularity@social_conservative } #Range from 0-1
		multiply_temp_variable = { YUN_whampoa_coup_mission_timer_change_temp_var = -100 } #Range from 0-100
		round_temp_variable = YUN_whampoa_coup_mission_timer_change_temp_var
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = YUN_whampoa_coup_mission_timer_change_temp_var
			min = -50
			max = -10
		}
		add_days_mission_timeout = {
			mission = YUN_The_Whampoa_Coup_mission
			days = YUN_whampoa_coup_mission_timer_change_temp_var
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.lategame.421 option YUN.lategame.421.c"
		name = YUN.lategame.421.c #The bickering groups on the left find no real direction.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					market_liberal > party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat
					social_democrat > party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat
					national_populist > party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = YUN_KMT_hu_hanmin_crisis_left_phase_2_tt
		set_temp_variable = { YUN_combined_leftist_popularity_temp_var = ROOT.party_popularity@totalist }
		add_to_temp_variable = { YUN_combined_leftist_popularity_temp_var = ROOT.party_popularity@syndicalist }
		add_to_temp_variable = { YUN_combined_leftist_popularity_temp_var = ROOT.party_popularity@radical_socialist }
		add_to_temp_variable = { YUN_combined_leftist_popularity_temp_var = ROOT.party_popularity@social_democrat }
		add_to_temp_variable = { YUN_combined_leftist_popularity_temp_var = ROOT.party_popularity@social_liberal }

		set_temp_variable = { YUN_PSC_delegate_change_temp_var = YUN_combined_leftist_popularity_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { YUN_PSC_delegate_change_temp_var = -0.25 } #Soc Dem makes this decision potentially a lot so gonna guage it a bit so its only a quarter.
		YUN_KMT_hu_hanmin_crisis_PSC_delegates_effect = yes
		set_temp_variable = { YUN_CCC_delegate_change_temp_var = YUN_combined_leftist_popularity_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { YUN_CCC_delegate_change_temp_var = 0.25 } #Soc Dem makes this decision potentially a lot so gonna guage it a bit so its only a quarter.
		YUN_KMT_hu_hanmin_crisis_CCC_delegates_effect = yes
		set_temp_variable = { YUN_whampoa_coup_mission_timer_change_temp_var = YUN_combined_leftist_popularity_temp_var } #Range from 0-1
		multiply_temp_variable = { YUN_whampoa_coup_mission_timer_change_temp_var = 100 } #Range from 0-100
		round_temp_variable = YUN_whampoa_coup_mission_timer_change_temp_var
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = YUN_whampoa_coup_mission_timer_change_temp_var
			min = 10
			max = 50
		}
		add_days_mission_timeout = {
			mission = YUN_The_Whampoa_Coup_mission
			days = YUN_whampoa_coup_mission_timer_change_temp_var
		}
	}

country_event = { #Hu Ruoyu Marches on Kunming
	id = YUN.lategame.511
	title = YUN.lategame.511.t
	desc = YUN.lategame.511.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_YUN_hu_ruoyu_1
	is_triggered_only = yes #TRIGGERED BY EFFECT: YUN_KMT_satellite_civil_war_winner_effect

	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			YUN_li_peitian = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			YUN_hu_ruoyu = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			YUN_lu_han = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }

			YUN_UPC_set_initial_parties = yes
			YUN_transition_to_NPA_army_tree_effect = yes
			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_hu_ruoyu
				ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = YUN_hu_ruoyu_clique_party_long
				name = YUN_hu_ruoyu_clique_party
			}
			activate_advisor = YUN_lu_han_sic
			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_lu_han
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = YUN_lu_han_clique_party_long
				name = YUN_lu_han_clique_party
			}
			set_country_flag = YUN_NPA_satellite_narrative_flag

			if = {
				limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = YUN_SCPC_KMT }
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes #Just in case the YUN_KMT cosmetic tag isn't already dropped.
				set_cosmetic_tag = YUN_SCPC_UPC
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = YUN_KMT }
				#Don't drop SCPC
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.lategame.511 option YUN.lategame.511.a"
		name = YUN.lategame.511.a #Yunnan returns to reaction.
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = no #No new elections until post unification tree
		}
		#Transfer a good chunk of Auth Dem Popularity over to Pat Aut
		add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = 0.20 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = -0.20 }
		YUN_long_yun = { retire = yes }
		YUN_li_peiyan = { retire = yes }
		YUN_li_peitian = { retire = yes }
		YUN_YSP_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_3AL_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_CEC_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_PSC_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_3AR_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_CCC_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_WPC_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_BSS_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_transition_to_NPA_pop_support_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = CHI_zhang_bojun }
			CHI_zhang_Bojun = { retire = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = YUN_gu_zhenglun }
			YUN_gu_zhenglun = { retire = yes }
		}

		YUN_TJY_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = YUN.lategame.890 days = 320 random_days = 80 } #Hu and Lu Square Off
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes

			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_tang_xiaoying
				ideology = social_conservative_subtype
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = focus_tree_will_change_tt
	}
}

		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					check_variable = { YUN.party_popularity@social_conservative > YUN.party_popularity@social_democrat }
					check_variable = { YUN.party_popularity@social_conservative > YUN.party_popularity@radical_socialist }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_KMT_path option = YUN_KMT_PATH_RADSOC }
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_KMT_path option = YUN_KMT_PATH_SOCDEM }

				}
			}
		}
		#For every non-Soc Con popularity in YUN, costs 0.50 pp (max 50 since YUN is peripherary).
		set_temp_variable = { YUN_pp_loss_temp_var = 1 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { YUN_pp_loss_temp_var = YUN.party_popularity@social_conservative }

			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0

					check_variable = { YUN.party_popularity@social_democrat > YUN.party_popularity@radical_socialist }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {

			YUN = { is_subject_of = CHI }
		}
		#For every non-Rad Soc popularity in YUN, costs 0.50 pp (max 50 since YUN is peripherary).
		set_temp_variable = { YUN_pp_loss_temp_var = 1 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { YUN_pp_loss_temp_var = YUN.party_popularity@radical_socialist }
		multiply_temp_variable = { YUN_pp_loss_temp_var = -50 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = CHN_deduct_pp_relative_to_non_ideology_in_country_tt
			IDEOLOGY = radical_socialist_coloured COUNTRY = "[YUN.GetNameDef]"
		}
		add_political_power = YUN_pp_loss_temp_var
		custom_effect_tooltip = YUN_chen_cheng_warning_tt
		YUN = { country_event = { id = YUN.lategame.523 days = 5 } }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = YUN.lategame.530 #The Central Government Collapses (YUN-KMT Variant)

	desc = YUN.lategame.530.d

	is_triggered_only = yes #triggered by [ON ACTION]: on_capitulation of YUN's overlord

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = YUN_phase_4_begins_flag
			end_coalition = yes

			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes

			YUN_hu_ruoyu = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			YUN_lu_han = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
		}
	}

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.lategame.530 option YUN.lategame.530.a"

		}

		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = -0.20 }

		YUN_long_yun = { retire = yes }
		YUN_li_peiyan = { retire = yes }
		YUN_li_peitian = { retire = yes }
		YUN_YSP_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_3AL_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_CEC_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_PSC_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_3AR_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_CCC_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_WPC_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_BSS_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_transition_to_NPA_pop_support_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = CHI_zhang_bojun }
			CHI_zhang_Bojun = { retire = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = YUN_gu_zhenglun }
			YUN_gu_zhenglun = { retire = yes }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = focus_tree_will_change_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = YUN.lategame.890 days = 320 random_days = 80 } #Hu and Lu Square Off
			YUN_transition_to_NPA_army_tree_effect = yes
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes

				name = YUN_hu_ruoyu_clique_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_lu_han
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = YUN_lu_han_clique_party_long
				name = YUN_lu_han_clique_party
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = YUN_SCPC_KMT }
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes #Just in case the YUN_KMT cosmetic tag isn't already dropped.
				set_cosmetic_tag = YUN_SCPC_UPC
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = YUN_KMT }
				#Don't drop SCPC
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			}
		}
	}

		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = -0.20 }

		YUN_long_yun = { retire = yes }
		YUN_li_peiyan = { retire = yes }
		YUN_li_peitian = { retire = yes }
		YUN_YSP_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_3AL_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_CEC_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_PSC_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_3AR_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_CCC_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_WPC_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_BSS_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_transition_to_NPA_pop_support_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = CHI_zhang_bojun }
			CHI_zhang_Bojun = { retire = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = YUN_gu_zhenglun }
			YUN_gu_zhenglun = { retire = yes }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = focus_tree_will_change_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = YUN.lategame.890 days = 320 random_days = 80 } #Hu and Lu Square Off
			YUN_transition_to_NPA_army_tree_effect = yes
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			YUN_li_peitian = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			complete_national_focus = YUN_as_the_flowers_bloom
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = YUN_hu_ruoyu_clique_party_long
				name = YUN_hu_ruoyu_clique_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_lu_han
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = YUN_lu_han_clique_party_long
				name = YUN_lu_han_clique_party
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = YUN_SCPC_KMT }
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes #Just in case the YUN_KMT cosmetic tag isn't already dropped.
				set_cosmetic_tag = YUN_SCPC_UPC
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = YUN_KMT }
				#Don't drop SCPC
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

				long_name = YUN_lu_han_clique_party_long
				name = YUN_lu_han_clique_party
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = YUN_SCPC_KMT }
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes #Just in case the YUN_KMT cosmetic tag isn't already dropped.
				set_cosmetic_tag = YUN_SCPC_UPC
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = YUN_KMT }
				#Don't drop SCPC
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.lategame.710 option YUN.lategame.710.a"
		name = YUN.lategame.710.a #Hu’s finally had his revenge.
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = no #No new elections until post unification tree
		}
		YUN_long_yun = { retire = yes }
		YUN_li_peiyan = { retire = yes }
		YUN_li_peitian = { retire = yes }
		YUN_YSP_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_3AL_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_CEC_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_PSC_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_3AR_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_CCC_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_WPC_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_BSS_purge_characters_minus_leaders_effect = yes
		YUN_transition_to_NPA_pop_support_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = CHI_zhang_bojun }
			CHI_zhang_Bojun = { retire = yes }
		}

country_event = { #Telegram From Kunming
	id = YUN.lategame.720
	title = YUN.lategame.720.t
	desc = YUN.lategame.720.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_YUN_tang_jiyao_3
	is_triggered_only = yes #TRIGGERED BY [EVENT]: YUN.lategame.703.b for UPC

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.lategame.720 option YUN.lategame.720.a"
		name = YUN.lategame.720.a #Send a response ordering Tang Jiyao to stand down and begin talks.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					check_variable = { YUN.party_popularity@social_democrat > YUN.party_popularity@social_conservative }
					#AI will take this if has game rules set
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_UPC_path option = YUN_UPC_PATH_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_UPC_path option = YUN_UPC_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_UPC_path option = YUN_UPC_XIAOYING_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		#For every non-Soc Dem popularity in YUN, costs 0.50 pp (max 50 since YUN is peripherary).
		set_temp_variable = { YUN_pp_loss_temp_var = 1 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { YUN_pp_loss_temp_var = YUN.party_popularity@social_democrat }
		multiply_temp_variable = { YUN_pp_loss_temp_var = -50 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = CHN_deduct_pp_relative_to_non_ideology_in_country_tt
			IDEOLOGY = social_democrat_coloured COUNTRY = "[YUN.GetNameDef]"
		}
		add_political_power = YUN_pp_loss_temp_var
		custom_effect_tooltip = YUN_cun_shusheng_warning_tt
		YUN = { country_event = { id = YUN.lategame.721 days = 5 } } #[UPC.Capital.GetCapitalVictoryPointName] Orders Tang to Stand Down
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.lategame.720 option YUN.lategame.720.b"
		name = YUN.lategame.720.b #Send a response recognising Tang’s authority and asking for negotiations.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					check_variable = { YUN.party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat > YUN.party_popularity@social_democrat }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0

				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_UPC_path option = YUN_UPC_PATH_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_UPC_path option = YUN_UPC_PATH_MARLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_UPC_path option = YUN_UPC_XIAOYING_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		#For every non-Auth Dem popularity in YUN, costs 0.50 pp (max 50 since YUN is peripherary).
		set_temp_variable = { YUN_pp_loss_temp_var = 1 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { YUN_pp_loss_temp_var = YUN.party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat }
		multiply_temp_variable = { YUN_pp_loss_temp_var = -50 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = CHN_deduct_pp_relative_to_non_ideology_in_country_tt
			IDEOLOGY = authoritarian_democrat_coloured COUNTRY = "[YUN.GetNameDef]"
		}
		add_political_power = YUN_pp_loss_temp_var
		custom_effect_tooltip = YUN_tang_jiyao_warning_tt
		YUN = { country_event = { id = YUN.lategame.722 days = 5 } } #[UPC.Capital.GetCapitalVictoryPointName] Reaffirms Tang’s Authority
	}

			if = {
				limit = { is_subject = yes }

		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = YUN.lategame.801 #The [GetYear] Political Conference
	title = YUN.lategame.801.t
	desc = YUN.lategame.801.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_YUN_NPA_three_contenders

	is_triggered_only = yes #Fired 7 days after [EVENT]: YUN.lategame.800 OR YUN.lategame.811 OR YUN.lategame.812

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "KR_Event_Logging;YUN GAME PROGRESS - YUN NPA Reaches Beijing"
			set_country_flag = YUN_phase_4_begins_flag
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			#Devastation effects since we're in phase IV
			CHN_setup_lategame_debuffs_effect = yes
			YUN_long_yun = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			YUN_li_peitian = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			YUN_hu_ruoyu = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			YUN_lu_han = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.lategame.801 option YUN.lategame.801.a"
		name = YUN.lategame.801.a #The army sways or intimidates civilian leaders into compliance.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					check_variable = { YUN.party_popularity@paternal_autocrat > YUN.party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_NPA_path option = YUN_NPA_PATH_LONG_YUN_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_NPA_path option = YUN_NPA_PATH_LONG_YUN_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		#Inform the player if they are forced into a coup because their popularity is too high.
		custom_effect_tooltip = YUN_NPA_guranteed_hu_coup_warning_tt
		#Deduct any PP
		set_temp_variable = { YUN_pp_loss_temp_var = 1 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { YUN_pp_loss_temp_var = YUN.party_popularity@paternal_autocrat }
		multiply_temp_variable = { YUN_pp_loss_temp_var = -100 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = CHN_deduct_pp_relative_to_non_ideology_in_country_tt
			IDEOLOGY = paternal_autocrat_coloured COUNTRY = "[YUN.GetNameDef]"
		}
		add_political_power = YUN_pp_loss_temp_var
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = no #No new elections until post unification tree
		}
		YUN_long_yun = { retire = yes }
		YUN_li_peiyan = { retire = yes }
		YUN_li_peitian = { retire = yes }
		#Purge all of Tang Jiyao's people that we don't want
		YUN_wang_jiexiu = { retire = yes }
		YUN_wu_xuexian = { retire = yes }
		YUN_sun_du = { retire = yes }
		YUN_chen_weigeng = { retire = yes }
		YUN_tang_jilin = { retire = yes }
		YUN_xi_ziqiang = { retire = yes }

		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_hu_ruoyu
				ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
			}
			activate_advisor = YUN_lu_han_sic
			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_lu_han
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = YUN_lu_han_clique_party_long
				name = YUN_lu_han_clique_party
			}
			news_event = { id = YUN.lategame.802 days = 1 } #Long Yun Toppled in a Coup
			country_event = { id = YUN.lategame.890 days = 320 random_days = 80 } #Hu and Lu Square Off
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.lategame.801 option YUN.lategame.801.b"
		name = YUN.lategame.801.b #The coup falls apart as the administration closes ranks behind Long.
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				#Rig it if you have game rules
				has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_NPA_path option = YUN_NPA_PATH_LONG_YUN_PATAUT }
				has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_NPA_path option = YUN_NPA_PATH_LONG_YUN_AUTDEM }
				#Normal triggers
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = YUN_NPA_beijing_endorsed_coup_flag
						paternal_autocrat > 0.50
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_NPA_path option = YUN_NPA_PATH_LONG_YUN_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_NPA_path option = YUN_NPA_PATH_LONG_YUN_AUTDEM }
					check_variable = { YUN.party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat > YUN.party_popularity@paternal_autocrat }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_NPA_path option = YUN_NPA_PATH_HU_RUOYU_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_NPA_path option = YUN_NPA_PATH_LU_HAN_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		#Punish Players for going against master's wishes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = YUN_NPA_beijing_endorsed_coup_flag }
			add_stability = -0.20
			add_war_support = -0.20
			custom_effect_tooltip = YUN_NPA_going_against_masters_wishes_tt
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = FROM
				modifier = KR_outraged
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = -0.10
			add_war_support = -0.10
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			elections_allowed = no #No new elections until post unification tree
		}
		#Purge Hu Ruoyu's Clique
		YUN_hu_ruoyu = { retire = yes }
		YUN_li_xuanting = { retire = yes }
		YUN_zhang_ruji = { retire = yes }
		YUN_wang_weiyu = { retire = yes }
		YUN_wang_ruwei = { retire = yes }
		#Long Yun's treacherous advisors
		YUN_lu_han = { retire = yes }
		YUN_zhang_chong = { retire = yes }
		hidden_effect = {
			YUN_li_peitian = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_long_yun
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
			activate_advisor = YUN_li_peitian_sic
			news_event = { id = YUN.lategame.803 days = 1 } #Long Yun Purges His Generals
			country_event = { id = YUN.lategame.860 days = 320 random_days = 80 } #Long Yun’s Ambition
		}
	}
	after = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = focus_tree_will_change_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_NPA_path option = YUN_NPA_PATH_LONG_YUN_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_NPA_path option = YUN_NPA_PATH_LONG_YUN_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_NPA_path option = YUN_NPA_PATH_HU_RUOYU_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_NPA_path option = YUN_NPA_PATH_LU_HAN_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHN_game_rule_rigged_warning_tt
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Yunnan Rises Again
	id = YUN.lategame.840
	title = YUN.lategame.840.t
	desc = YUN.lategame.840.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_YUN_tang_jiyao_painting
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by FOCUS: YUN_the_unexpected_development

	option = { #They will not stop us this time!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.lategame.840 option YUN.lategame.840.a"
		name = YUN.lategame.840.a
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;YUN GAME PROGRESS - YUN NPA Forms a Government"
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = YUN_hu_ruoyu ruling_only = yes } } #Manual override
			set_country_flag = china_is_potential_government
			save_global_event_target_as = npa_leader
			set_cosmetic_tag = national_protection_alliance
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_china = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							is_subject_of = PREV.PREV
							china_is_governorate = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_PREV = no }
					add_to_array = { PREV.china_government_claims = THIS }
					add_claim_by = PREV
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_variable = ambition_area_@PREV } }
					add_to_array = { PREV.china_government_ambitions = THIS }
					set_variable = { ambition_area_@PREV = 1 }
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_china_claim_area = yes
						is_claim_or_core_of_PREV = no
						NOT = { has_variable = ambition_area_@PREV }
					}
					add_to_array = { PREV.china_government_ambitions = THIS }
					set_variable = { ambition_area_@PREV = 1 }
				}
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = china_provisional_capital }
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_potential_national_government = yes
		}
		YUN = {
			set_capital = { state = 592 } #Guangzhou
			add_state_core = 592
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = YUN.lategame.841 #The National Protection Alliance Reforms
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Nationalist Government Falters
	id = YUN.endgame.010
	title = YUN.endgame.010.t
	desc = {
		text = YUN.endgame.010.d.kmt
		trigger = {
			china_alignment_right_kuomintang = yes
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = YUN.endgame.010.d.shxgmj
		trigger = {
			tag = SHX
			has_country_leader = {
				character = SHX_feng_yuxiang
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = YUN.endgame.010.d.shxyan
		trigger = {
			tag = SHX
			has_country_leader = {
				character = SHX_yan_xishan
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = YUN.endgame.010.d.generic
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = SHX
				china_alignment_right_kuomintang = yes
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_YUN_NRA_soldiers_3

	is_triggered_only = yes #Event: YUN.endgame.000, YUN.endgame.001, YUN.endgame.100

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.endgame.010 option YUN.endgame.010.a"
		name = YUN.endgame.010.a #[FROM.GetLeader] is a corrupt tyrant and must be brought low!
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		#Penalty depending on your alignment - PP and Stab already deducted earlier.
		if = {
			limit = { china_same_alignment_as_FROM = yes } #PREV is GXC
			add_command_power = -100
			add_war_support = -0.10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = yes } #LKMT or Republicans
			add_command_power = -50
			add_war_support = -0.05
		}
		else = {
			#Everyone else
			add_command_power = -30
			add_war_support = -0.03
		}

		#Break the Puppetship
		china_break_puppet_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { can_declare_war_on = FROM }
			create_wargoal = {
				target = FROM
				type = topple_government
			}
		}

		#Inform GXC
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_chinese_tag = yes }
				country_event = { id = YUN.endgame.011 days = 1 } #[FROM.GetLeader] Contests the Election!
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.endgame.010 option YUN.endgame.010.b"
		name = YUN.endgame.010.b #[FROM.Capital.GetCapitalVictoryPointName] can say what they want about centralisation, but we will go at our own pace.
		trigger = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = no }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		add_political_power = 15
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.endgame.010 option YUN.endgame.010.c"
		name = YUN.endgame.010.c #It is time we bring our province into the fold. (Switch to [YUN.GetNameDef])
		trigger = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = yes }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		effect_tooltip = { china_integrate_ally_effect = yes }
		YUN = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHN_done_our_patriotic_duty_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			YUN = {
				country_event = { id = china_events.18 days = 3 } #[FROM.Adjective] Nationalists Return to the Fold
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Federalism Realised?
	id = YUN.endgame.304
	title = YUN.endgame.304.t
	desc = {
		text = YUN.endgame.304.d_hnn
		trigger = {
			tag = HNN
			china_alignment_federalists = yes
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = YUN.endgame.304.d_szc
		trigger = {
			tag = SZC
			china_alignment_federalists = yes
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = YUN.endgame.304.d_generic
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					china_alignment_federalists = yes
					OR = {
						tag = YUN
						tag = HNN
						tag = SZC
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_GXC_guangxi_troops_3

	is_triggered_only = yes #[EVENT]: YUN.endgame.303

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.endgame.304 option YUN.endgame.304.a"
		name = YUN.endgame.304.a #When you shoot for the king...
		trigger = {
			CHN_has_civil_war_prep_trigger = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		#Penalty depending on your alignment - PP and Stab already deducted earlier.
		if = {
			limit = { china_same_alignment_as_FROM = yes } #PREV is YUN
			add_command_power = -100
			add_war_support = -0.10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = yes } #Republicans
			add_command_power = -50
			add_war_support = -0.05
		}
		else = {
			#Everyone else
			add_command_power = -30
			add_war_support = -0.03
		}

		#Break the Puppetship
		china_break_puppet_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { can_declare_war_on = FROM }
			create_wargoal = {
				target = FROM
				type = topple_government
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_chinese_tag = yes }
				country_event = { id = YUN.endgame.305 days = 1 } #[FROM.GetLeader] Resists Nationalisation
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.endgame.304 option YUN.endgame.304.b"
		name = YUN.endgame.304.b #Perhaps he'll stay true to his word?
		trigger = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = no }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		add_political_power = 15
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.endgame.304 option YUN.endgame.304.c"
		name = YUN.endgame.304.c #Can hardly get far sitting on the sidelines! (Switch to [UPC.GetNameDef])
		trigger = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = yes }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		effect_tooltip = { china_integrate_ally_effect = yes }
		YUN = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHN_done_our_patriotic_duty_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			YUN = {
				country_event = { id = china_events.190 days = 3 } #[FROM.Adjective] Federalists Join Our Government
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Democracy’s Martyrs
	id = YUN.endgame.323
	title = YUN.endgame.323.t
	desc = YUN.endgame.323.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_YUN_wen_yiduo_scarf

	is_triggered_only = yes #Fired by [EVENT] YUN.endgame.320 OR YUN.endgame.321 OR YUN.endgame.322
	fire_only_once = yes #Avoids allowing it trigger multiple times

	option = { #[UPC_GetSTAPartyLeader] has won, but at a terrible cost.
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.endgame.323 option YUN.endgame.323.a"
		name = YUN.endgame.323.a
		YUN_wen_yiduo = { kill_character = yes }
		UPC_sub_enthusiasm_mega_effect = yes
		UPC_end_federalist_democracy_effect = yes
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes #So natural pace of elections will still happen and you get the auth dem elections event.
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = YUN
					has_country_flag = YUN_UPC_satellite_election_path_flag
				}
				promote_character = {
					character = YUN_tang_xiaoying
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					tag = YUN
					NOT = { has_country_flag = YUN_UPC_satellite_election_path_flag }
				}
				promote_character = {
					character = YUN_tang_jiyao
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
				}
			}
			activate_advisor = YUN_zhang_weihan_sic
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = YUN_UPC_popular_support_rule_of_the_expertocracy }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = YUN_UPC_popular_support_rule_of_the_expertocracy
					add_idea = YUN_UPC_popular_support_5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = YUN_UPC_popular_support_anathema_to_popular_revolt }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = YUN_UPC_popular_support_anathema_to_popular_revolt
					add_idea = YUN_UPC_popular_support_5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = YUN_UPC_popular_support_grand_republican_statesman }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = YUN_UPC_popular_support_grand_republican_statesman
					add_idea = YUN_UPC_popular_support_5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = YUN_UPC_popular_support_arbiters_of_the_nation }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = YUN_UPC_popular_support_arbiters_of_the_nation
					add_idea = YUN_UPC_popular_support_5
				}
			}
			#Uncomplete focuses
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = YUN_the_fight_for_human_rights
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = YUN_the_fight_for_human_rights
					uncomplete_children = no #Avoid removing shared focuses
					refund_political_power = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = YUN_ending_the_political_chaos
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = YUN_ending_the_political_chaos
					uncomplete_children = no #Avoid removing shared focuses
					refund_political_power = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = YUN_cultivating_liberal_nationalism
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = YUN_cultivating_liberal_nationalism
					uncomplete_children = yes
					refund_political_power = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = YUN_third_way_economics
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = YUN_third_way_economics
					uncomplete_children = yes
					refund_political_power = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = YUN_zhang_taiyans_federation
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = YUN_zhang_taiyans_federation
					uncomplete_children = yes
					refund_political_power = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Finishing the Mission
	id = YUN.endgame.600
	title = YUN.endgame.600.t
	desc = YUN.endgame.600.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SZC_sichuan_soldiers_1

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by [DECISION]: china_declare_unification

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = YUN_phase_5_begins_flag
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			country_event = { id = YUN.endgame.601 days = 3 } #Consequences of Economic Misamanagement

			CHI = {
				CHI_wang_jingwei = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
				CHI_chen_duxiu = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			}
			QIE = {
				QIE_wu_xianzi = {
					CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_ideology = social_democrat_subtype
						}
						promote_character = social_democrat_subtype
					}
					else = {
						add_country_leader_role = {
							country_leader = {
								desc = QIE_wu_xianzi_leader_desc
								ideology = social_democrat_subtype
								traits = { CHN_beiyang_aligned }
							}
							promote_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}

			#Organize Endgame Parties
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = totalist
				long_name = CHN_radicals_party_long
				name = CHN_radicals_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_assorted_leaders
				ideology = totalist_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = syndicalist
				long_name = CHN_CSP_party_long
				name = CHN_CSP_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = CHI_chen_duxiu
				ideology = syndicalist_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				long_name = CHN_KMT_party_long
				name = CHN_KMT_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = CHI_wang_jingwei
				ideology = radical_socialist_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = CHN_DCP_party_long
				name = CHN_DCP_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = QIE_wu_xianzi
				ideology = social_democrat_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				long_name = CHN_FCDP_party_long
				name = CHN_FCDP_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_luo_longji
				ideology = social_liberal_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				long_name = CHN_republicans_party_long
				name = CHN_republicans_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_assorted_leaders
				ideology = market_liberal_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				long_name = CHN_GRA_party_long
				name = CHN_GRA_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_tang_xiaoying
				ideology = social_conservative_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = national_populist
				long_name = CHN_YCP_party_long
				name = CHN_YCP_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_liao_xingchao
				ideology = national_populist_subtype
			}

			#Okay Path Specific Now
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_leader = { character = YUN_hu_ruoyu }
						has_country_leader = { character = YUN_lu_han }
					}
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					long_name = YUN_lu_han_clique_party_long
					name = YUN_lu_han_clique_party
				}
				promote_character = {
					character = YUN_lu_han
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					long_name = YUN_hu_ruoyu_clique_national_party_long
					name = YUN_hu_ruoyu_clique_party
				}
				promote_character = {
					character = YUN_hu_ruoyu
					ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					long_name = YUN_long_yun_clique_national_party_long
					name = YUN_long_yun_clique_party
				}
				promote_character = {
					character = YUN_long_yun
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
				}
				#May switch Long Yun to pat aut later
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					long_name = CHN_regionalists_party_long
					name = CHN_regionalists_party
				}
				promote_character = {
					character = YUN_assorted_leaders
					ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.endgame.600 option YUN.endgame.600.a"
		name = YUN.endgame.600.a #We must build a nation from scraps.

			if = {
				limit = { is_subject = no }
				news_event = china_events.363 #Yunnan Warlords Unite China
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = YUN.endgame.604.a #
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }

		#No need for penalty depending on alignment since this an NPA tag. will do baseline penalty.
		add_command_power = -30
		add_war_support = -0.03

		#Break the Puppetship
		china_break_puppet_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { can_declare_war_on = FROM }
			create_wargoal = {
				target = FROM
				type = topple_government
			}
		}

		#Inform GXC
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_chinese_tag = yes }
				country_event = { id = YUN.endgame.605 days = 1 } #[FROM.GetLeader] Declares \"Independence\"
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.endgame.604 option YUN.endgame.604.b"
		name = YUN.endgame.604.b #
		trigger = { china_compatible_alignment_to_FROM = no }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		add_political_power = 15
	}
}

country_event = { #[FROM.GetLeader] Declares \"Independence\"
	id = YUN.endgame.605
	title = YUN.endgame.605.t
	desc = {
		text = YUN.endgame.605.d.shxgmj
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = YUN
				has_country_leader = {
					character = SHX_feng_yuxiang
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = YUN.endgame.605.d.shxyan
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = SHX
				has_country_leader = {
					character = SHX_yan_xishan
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = YUN.endgame.605.d.generic
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					tag = SHX
				}
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHN_warlord_cavalry

	is_triggered_only = yes #Event: YUN.endgame.604

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.endgame.605 option YUN.endgame.605.a"
		name = YUN.endgame.605.a #The Dian Army is but undefeatable!
		trigger = { tag = YUN }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = { can_declare_war_on = FROM }
			create_wargoal = {
				target = FROM
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.endgame.605 option YUN.endgame.605.b"
		name = YUN.endgame.605.b #Once more into the brink.
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = YUN } }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
}

#LYC Endgame Events (630-659):
country_event = { #The National Protection Cabinet
	id = YUN.endgame.630
	title = YUN.endgame.630.t
	desc = YUN.endgame.630.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_YUN_UPC_PGP

	is_triggered_only = yes #Fired 3 days after [FOCUS] All Under the King

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			#In case this didn't happen already
			YUN_long_yun = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			YUN_li_peitian = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			YUN_wang_dong = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
		}
	}

	option = { #The Li brothers are our preferred choice.
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.endgame.630 option YUN.endgame.630.a"
		name = YUN.endgame.630.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_NPA_path option = YUN_NPA_PATH_LONG_YUN_AUTDEM }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			save_current_party_popularities = yes
			set_temp_variable = { GXC_new_authdem_value = saved_popularities^8 } #Current Pat Aut
			set_temp_variable = { GXC_new_pataut_value = saved_popularities^7 } #Current Auth Dem
			set_popularities = {
				totalist = saved_popularities^0
				syndicalist = saved_popularities^1
				radical_socialist = saved_popularities^2
				social_democrat = saved_popularities^3
				social_liberal = saved_popularities^4
				market_liberal = saved_popularities^5
				social_conservative = saved_popularities^6
				authoritarian_democrat = GXC_new_authdem_value
				paternal_autocrat = GXC_new_pataut_value
				national_populist = saved_popularities^9
			}

			#May switch in a later event.
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = CHN_regionalists_party_long
				name = CHN_regionalists_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_assorted_leaders
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = YUN_long_yun_clique_national_party_long
				name = YUN_long_yun_clique_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_long_yun
				ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
			}
			activate_advisor = YUN_li_peitian_sic
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = YUN.endgame.630.a_tt
		set_politics = { ruling_party = paternal_autocrat }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.10
		}
	}
	option = { #The Wang brothers are a necessary one.
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event YUN.endgame.630 option YUN.endgame.630.b"
		name = YUN.endgame.630.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = YUN_NPA_path option = YUN_NPA_PATH_LONG_YUN_PATAUT }
			}
		}
		set_politics = { ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = {
				character = YUN_long_yun
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
			activate_advisor = YUN_wang_dong_sic
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Lu Han’s Uprising
	id = YUN.endgame.660
	title = YUN.endgame.660.t
	desc = YUN.endgame.660.d

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			#In case this didn't happen already
			YUN_hu_ruoyu = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			YUN_lu_han = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }
			YUN_zhou_zhongyue = { CHN_recruit_character_effect = yes }

				ideology = authoritarian_democrat

		}

				long_name = CHN_regionalists_party_long
				name = CHN_regionalists_party
			}
